<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var origUrl = window.location.href.split('?')[0];

		if(window.location.pathname == '/giving') //explicit rewrite rule requested by client
		{
			origUrl = location.protocol + "//" + window.location.hostname + '/get-involved/donate';
		}

		if(window.location.pathname == '/') //default homepage URL
		{
			origUrl = location.protocol + "//" + window.location.hostname + '/home';
		}

        var callbackUrl = origUrl + "/Callback";
        var triggerCallback = callbackUrl.indexOf("/Sitefinity") < 0 //not CMS
            && callbackUrl.indexOf("/product/") < 0 //not product details
            && callbackUrl.indexOf("/Action/Edit") < 0 //edit mode
        if (triggerCallback == true) {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                cache: false,
                url: callbackUrl,
                contentType: "application/json;charset=utf-8",
                async: false,
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.indexOf("is-logged-out") >= 0
                        && origUrl.indexOf("/account-management/log-in") < 0
                        && $("#IsLoginRequired").val().toLowerCase() == "true")
                        window.location.href = "/account-management/log-in";
                    else
                        $("#LoginStatusSection").html(result);
                },
                error: function (error) {
                    console.log("Callback Error:");
                    console.log(error)
                }
            });
        }

        $("#LoginStatusSection").show();
    });
</script>
            
        </div>
    </div>
    <div class="sf_colsOut sf_2cols_2_50">
        <div id="Content_Nav_T81990DB1040_Col01" class="sf_colsIn sf_2cols_2in_50">            
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
    $(document).ready(function () {
        var origUrl = window.location.href.split('?')[0];

		if(window.location.pathname == '/giving') //explicit rewrite rule requested by client
		{
			origUrl = location.protocol + "//" + window.location.hostname + '/get-involved/donate';
		}

		if(window.location.pathname == '/') //default homepage URL
		{
			origUrl = location.protocol + "//" + window.location.hostname + '/home';
		}

        var callbackUrl = origUrl + "/Callback";
        var triggerCallback = callbackUrl.indexOf("/Sitefinity") < 0 //not CMS
            && callbackUrl.indexOf("/product/") < 0 //not product details
            && callbackUrl.indexOf("/Action/Edit") < 0 //edit mode
        if (triggerCallback == true) {
            $.ajax({
                type: "POST",
                cache: false,
                url: callbackUrl,
                contentType: "application/json;charset=utf-8",
                async: false,
                success: function (result) {
                    if (result.indexOf("is-logged-out") >= 0
                        && origUrl.indexOf("/account-management/log-in") < 0
                        && $("#IsLoginRequired").val().toLowerCase() == "true")
                        window.location.href = "/account-management/log-in";
                    else
                        $("#LoginStatusSection").html(result);
                },
                error: function (error) {
                    console.log("Callback Error:");
                    console.log(error)
                }
            });
        }

        $("#LoginStatusSection").show();
    });
</script>
